 When it comes to health, sugar is always treated like a villain
 lekin kai tareekon se yah phydemand bhi hoti he
 Although it is absolutely true that eating sugar increases weight but sugar is also necessary for staying healthy
 iske apane phaayde hai jinako nishchit taur par nazarandaaj nahin kiya ja saktaa:1
 If you need immediate energy for instant strength, then nothing is better than sugar
 khun main pahunchakar chini glucose main badal jaati he, jo chini kaa saralatam rup hota he
 The cells then absorb glucose and transmit energy
 aapako jaanakar hairaani hogi ki kai khilaadi turant thakaan mitaane ke liye apane saath sugar cubs rakhte hai
 2
 lo blad pressure waalon ke liegin logon ko loblad pressure kii shikaayat hoti haiunhen apane saath sugar cubs rakhane kii salaah di jaati he
 Eating this increases blood pressure
 agar aapako blike out (chalate-chalate ankhon ke aage andhera chaane) kii samasya he to isamen chini madadgaar he
 3
 dimag ke liehamaara dimag bina sugar ke kaam hi nahin kar saktaa
 a black out situation arises when the sugar supply to the brain stops

 depressant dur karne ke liedipressant ko dur karne main bhi sugar bahut madadgaar he
